   lobhadveṣābhibhūtānāṃ vyavahāraḥ pravartitaḥ // Brh_1,1.1 //	loBa-dveza-aBiBUtAnAm vyavahAraH pravartitaH // Brh_1,1.1 //
   prayacchec ced bhṛtiṃ svāmī bhṛtyānāṃ karma kurvatām /	prayacCet ced BRtim svAmI BRtyAnAm karma kurvatAm /
   na kurvanti ca bhṛtyāś cet tatra vādaḥ pravartate // Brh_1,1.2 //	na kurvanti ca BRtyAH ced tatra vAdaH pravartate // Brh_1,1.2 //
   hiṃsāṃ vā kurute kaś cid deyaṃ vā na prayacchati /	hiMsAm vA kurute kaH cit deyam vA na prayacCati /
   dve hi sthāne vivādasya tayor bahutarā gatiḥ // Brh_1,1.3 //	dve hi sTAne vivAdasya tayoH bahutarA gatiH // Brh_1,1.3 //
   yato dravyaṃ vinikrīya ṛṇārthaṃ caiva gṛhyate /	yatas dravyam vinikrIya RNa-arTam ca-eva gRhyate /
   tanmūlyam uttamarṇena vyavahāra iti smṛtaḥ // Brh_1,1.4 //	tad-mUlyam uttamarNena vyavahAraH iti smRtaH // Brh_1,1.4 //
   [Brh_1,1.1 rājaguṇāḥ]	[Brh_1,1.1 rAja-guNAH]
   guṇadharmān ato rājñaḥ kathayāmy anupūrvaśaḥ /	guNa-DarmAn atas rAjQaH kaTayAmi anupUrvaSas /
   dhanikarṇikasaṃdigdhau pratibhūlekhyasākṣiṇaḥ // Brh_1,1.5 //	Danika-RNika-saMdigDO pratiBU-leKya-sAkziNaH // Brh_1,1.5 //
   vicārayati yaḥ samyak tasyotpattiṃ nibodhata /	vicArayati yaH samyak tasya-utpattim niboData /
   somāgnyarkānilendrāṇāṃ vittāpattyor yamasya ca // Brh_1,1.6 //	soma-agni-arka-anila-indrANAm vitta-ApattyoH yamasya ca // Brh_1,1.6 //
   tejomātraṃ samuddhṛtya rājño mūrtir hi nirmitā /	tejaH-mAtram samudDRtya rAjQaH mUrtiH hi nirmitA /

   bhayād bhogāya kalpante svadharmān na calanti ca /	BayAt BogAya kalpante svaDarmAt na calanti ca /

   tasmād varṇāśramāṇāṃ tu netāsau nirmitaḥ purā /	tasmAt varNa-ASramANAm tu netA-asO nirmitaH purA /
   [Brh_1,1.2 vyavahārapadāni]	[Brh_1,1.2 vyavahAra-padAni]

   dvisaptako'rthamūlas tu hiṃsāmūlaś caturvidhaḥ /	dvi-saptakaH-arTa-mUlaH tu hiMsA-mUlaH caturviDaH /
   pāruṣye dve vadhaś caiva parastrīsaṃgrahas tathā // Brh_1,1.10 //	pAruzye dve vaDaH ca-eva para-strI-saMgrahaH taTA // Brh_1,1.10 //
   kusīdanidhideyād yaṃ saṃbhūyotthānam eva ca /	kusIda-niDi-deyAt yam saMBUya-utTAnam eva ca /
   bhṛtyadānam aśuśrūṣā bhūvādo 'svāmivikriyaḥ // Brh_1,1.11 //	BRtya-dAnam aSuSrUzA BUvAdaH asvAmi-vikriyaH // Brh_1,1.11 //
   krayavikrayānuśayaḥ samayātikramas tathā /	kraya-vikraya-anuSayaH samayA-atikramaH taTA /

   etāny arthasamutthāni padāni tu caturdaśa /	etAni arTa-samutTAni padAni tu caturdaSa /
   punar evaṃ prabhinnāni kriyābhedād anekadahā // Brh_1,1.13 //	punar evam praBinnAni kriyA-BedAt aneka-dahAH // Brh_1,1.13 //
   pāruṣye dve sāhasaṃ ca parastrīsaṃgrahas tathā /	pAruzye dve sAhasam ca para-strI-saMgrahaH taTA /
   hiṃsodbhavapadāny evaṃ catvāry āha bṛhaspatiḥ // Brh_1,1.14 //	hiMsA-udBava-padAni evam catvAri Aha bRhaspatiH // Brh_1,1.14 //
   hīnamadhyottamatvena prabhinnāni pṛthak pṛthak /	hIna-maDya-uttama-tvena praBinnAni pRTak pRTak /
   viśeṣa eṣāṃ nirdiṣṭaś caturṇām apy anukramāt // Brh_1,1.15 //	viSezaH ezAm nirdizwaH caturNAm api anukramAt // Brh_1,1.15 //
   padāny aṣṭādaśaitāni dharmaśāstroditāni tu /	padAni azwAdaSa-etAni Darma-SAstra-uditAni tu /

   pūrvapakṣaḥ smṛtaḥ pādo dvitīyas tūttaras tathā /	pUrvapakzaH smRtaH pAdaH dvitIyaH tu-uttaraH taTA /
   kriyāpādas tathā vācyaś caturtho nirṇayas tathā // Brh_1,1.17 //	kriyA-pAdaH taTA vAcyaH caturTaH nirNayaH taTA // Brh_1,1.17 //
   [Brh_1,1.3 dharmādicatuṣṭayabalābalam]	[Brh_1,1.3 Darma-Adi-catuzwaya-bala-abalam]

   vihāya caritācāraṃ yatra kuryāt punar nṛpaḥ /	vihAya carita-AcAram yatra kuryAt punar nRpaH /

   dharmaśāstrānusāreṇa sāmātyaḥ sa purohitaḥ /	Darma-SAstra-anusAreNa sa-amAtyaH sa purohitaH /

   krodhalobhavihīnas tu satyavādī jitendriyaḥ // Brh_1,1.22 //	kroDa-loBa-vihInaH tu satya-vAdI jita-indriyaH // Brh_1,1.22 //
   [Brh_1,1.4 dharmādhikaraṇam]	[Brh_1,1.4 Darma-aDikaraNam]
   saptaprakṛtikaṃ yat tu vijigīṣor areś ca yat /	sapta-prakRtikam yat tu vijigIzoH areH ca yat /

   catvāraḥ pṛthivīpālāḥ pṛthaṅmitraiḥ sahāṣṭakam /	catvAraH pRTivIpAlAH pRTak-mitrEH saha-azwakam /
   amātyādibhir ete ca jagaty akṣarasaṃhitāḥ // Brh_1,1.24 //	amAtya-AdiBiH ete ca jagati akzara-saMhitAH // Brh_1,1.24 //
   prātar utthāya nṛpatiḥ śaucaṃ kṛtvā vidhānataḥ /	prAtar utTAya nRpatiH SOcam kRtvA viDAnataH /

   [Brh_1,1.5 durgalakṣaṇam]	[Brh_1,1.5 durga-lakzaNam]

   [Brh_1,1.7 sabhāniveśanaprakāraḥ]	[Brh_1,1.7 saBA-niveSana-prakAraH]

   [Brh_1,1.8 sabhāprabhedāḥ]	[Brh_1,1.8 saBA-praBedAH]
   pratiṣṭhitāpratiṣṭhā ca mudritā śāsitā tathā /	pratizWita-apratizWA ca mudritA SAsitA taTA /

   pratiṣṭhitā pure grāme calā nāmāpratiṣṭhitā /	pratizWitA pure grAme calAH nAma-apratizWitA /

   [Brh_1,2.1 pakṣalakṣaṇam]	[Brh_1,2.1 pakza-lakzaNam]

   [Brh_1,3. uttaram]	[Brh_1,3. uttaram]

   [Brh_1,3.2 caturvidham uttaram]	[Brh_1,3.2 caturviDam uttaram]

   mithyā tat tu vijānīyād uttaraṃ vyavahārataḥ // Brh_1,3.17 //	miTyA tat tu vijAnIyAt uttaram vyavahArataH // Brh_1,3.17 //

   [Brh_1,4. kriyāpādaḥ]	[Brh_1,4. kriyA-pAdaH]

   nivāsaś ca vijñeyaḥ sākṣī likhitasaṃjñakaḥ // Brh_1,5.6 //	nivAsaH ca vijQeyaH sAkzI liKita-saMjQakaH // Brh_1,5.6 //

   āhūya yaḥ kṛtaḥ sākṣī ṛṇanyāsakriyādike [p.51] /	AhUya yaH kRtaH sAkzI RNa-nyAsa-kriyA-Adike [p.51] /

   [Brh_1,5.2 sākṣidoṣakathanaṃ duṣṭānāṃ daṇḍaś ca]	[Brh_1,5.2 sAkzi-doza-kaTanam duzwAnAm daNxaH ca]

   [Brh_1,6. likhitam]	[Brh_1,6. liKitam]

   [Brh_1,6.2 lekhyabhedāḥ]	[Br=-_1,6.2 leKya-BedAH]

   [Brh_1,10 ṛṇādānam]	[Brh_1,10 RNa-AdAnam]

   [Brh_1,20 vākpāruṣyam]	[Brh-_1,20 vAc-pAruzyam]

   [Brh_1,26.5 putravibhāgaḥ]	[Brh_1,26.5 putra-viBAgaH]

   saṃprītyā sādhanīyās te svārthahānyā chalena vā // Brh_1,26.142 //	saMprItyA sADanIyAH te sva-arTa-hAnyA Calena vA // Brh_1,26.142 //
   sāhasaṃ sthāvarasvāmyaṃ prāgvibhāgaś ca rikthinām /	sAhasam sTAvara-svAmyam prAk-viBAgaH ca rikTinAm /
   anumānena vijñeyaṃ na syur yatra ca sākṣiṇaḥ // Brh_1,26.143 //	anumAnena vijQeyam na syuH yatra ca sAkziNaH // Brh_1,26.143 //
   [Brh_1,26.14 vibhaktakriyā]	[Brh_1,26.14 viBakta-kriyA]
   teṣām etāḥ kriyā loke pravartante svarikthiṣu /	tezAm etAH kriyAH loke pravartante sva-rikTizu /
   vibhaktān avagaccheyur lekhyam apy antareṇa tān // Brh_1,26.144 //	viBaktAn avagacCeyuH leKyam api antareNa tAn // Brh_1,26.144 //
   avibhaktaiś ca kartavyā vaiśvadevādikāḥ kriyāḥ // Brh_1,26.145 //	aviBaktEH ca kartavyAH vESvadeva-AdikAH kriyAH // Brh_1,26.145 //
   balānubandhavyāghāta- hoḍhaṃ sāhasabhāvakam /	bala-anubanDa-vyAGAta hoXam sAhasa-BAvakam /
   svasya bhogaḥ sthāvarasya vibhāgasya pṛthagdhanam // Brh_1,26.146 //	svasya BogaH sTAvarasya viBAgasya pRTak-Danam // Brh_1,26.146 //
   pṛthagāyavyayadhanāḥ kusīdaṃ ca parasparam /	pRTak-Aya-vyaya-DanAH kusIdam ca parasparam /
   vaṇikpathaṃ ca ye kuryur vibhaktās te na saṃśayaḥ // Brh_1,26.147 //	vaNikpaTam ca ye kuryuH viBaktAH te na saMSayaH // Brh_1,26.147 //
   kāryam ucchrāvaṇālekhyaṃ vibhaktair bhrātṛbhir mithaḥ /	kAryam ucCrAvaNa-AleKyam viBaktEH BrAtRBiH miTas /
   sākṣiṇo vā virodhārthaṃ vibhajadbhir aninditāḥ // Brh_1,26.148 //	sAkziNaH vA viroDa-arTam viBajadBiH aninditAH // Brh_1,26.148 //
   yenāṃśo yādṛśo bhuktas tasya taṃ na vicālayet // Brh_1,26.149 //	yena-aMSaH yAdRSaH BuktaH tasya tam na vicAlayet // Brh_1,26.149 //
   [Brh_1,27 dyūtam]	[Brh_1,27 dyUtam]
   [Brh_1,27.]	[Brh-_1,27.]
   dyūtaṃ niṣiddhaṃ manunā satyaśaucadhanāpaham /	dyUtam nizidDam manunA satya-SOca-Dana-apaham /
   tat pravartitam anyais tu rājabhāgasamanvitam // Brh_1,27.1 //	tat pravartitam anyEH tu rAja-BAga-samanvitam // Brh_1,27.1 //
   sabhikādhiṣṭhitaṃ kāryaṃ taskarajñānahetunā /	saBika-aDizWitam kAryam taskara-jQAna-hetunA /
   eṣa eva vidhir jñeyaḥ prāṇidyūtasamāhvaye // Brh_1,27.2 //	ezaH eva viDiH jQeyaH prANi-dyUta-samAhvaye // Brh_1,27.2 //
   [Brh_1,27.1 sabhikavṛttiḥ]	[Brh_1,27.1 saBika-vRttiH]
   sabhiko grāhakas tatra dadyāj jetre nṛpāya ca /	saBikaH grAhakaH tatra dadyAt jetre nRpAya ca /
   rājavṛddhiḥ sakitavāt sabhikād daśakaṃ śatam // Brh_1,27.3 //	rAja-vRdDiH sa-kitavAt saBikAt daSakam Satam // Brh_1,27.3 //
   yathāsamayaṃ vā syāt . .... .... // Brh_1,27.4 //	yaTAsamayam vA syAt . .... .... // Brh_1,27.4 //
   [Brh_1,27.2 svāminor jayaparājayaḥ]	[Brh_1,27.2 svAminoH jaya-parAjayaH]
   dvandvayuddhena yaḥ kaścid avasādam avāpnuyāt /	dvandva-yudDena yaH kaScid avasAdam avApnuyAt /
   tat svāminā paṇo deyo yas tatra parikalpitaḥ // Brh_1,27.5 //	tat svAminA paNaH deyaH yaH tatra parikalpitaH // Brh_1,27.5 //
   rahojito 'nabhijñaś ca kūṭākṣaiḥ kapaṭena vā /	rahojitaH anaBijQaH ca kUwa-akzEH kapawena vA /
   mocyo 'bhijño 'pi sarvasvam jitaṃ sarvaṃ na dāpyate // Brh_1,27.6 //	mocyaH aBijQaH api sarva-svam jitam sarvam na dApyate // Brh_1,27.6 //
   [Brh_1,27.3 kūṭadyūtadaṇḍaḥ]	[Brh_1,27.3 kUwa-dyUta-daNxaH]
   kūṭākṣadevinaḥ pāpā rājabhāgaharāś ca ye /	kUwa-akza-devinaH pApAH rAja-BAga-harAH ca ye /
   gaṇanāvañcakāś caiva daṇḍyās te kitavāḥ smṛtāḥ // Brh_1,27.7 //	gaNanA-vaQcakAH ca-eva daNxyAH te kitavAH smRtAH // Brh_1,27.7 //
   grahaḥ prakāśaḥ kartavyo nirvāsyāḥ kūṭadevinaḥ /	grahaH prakASaH kartavyaH nirvAsyAH kUwa-devinaH /
   vyāpādane tu tatkārī vadhaṃ citram avāpnuyāt // Brh_1,27.8 //	vyApAdane tu tad-kArI vaDam citram avApnuyAt // Brh_1,27.8 //
   [Brh_1,27.4 saṃdigdhajayaparājayanirṇayaḥ]	[Brh_1,27.4 saMdigDa-jaya-parAjaya-nirNayaH]
   sa eva sākṣī saṃdigdhau sabhyaiś cānyais tribhir vṛtaḥ /	saH eva sAkzI saMdigDO saByEH ca-anyEH triBiH vRtaH /
   ubhayor api saṃdigdhaṃ kitavās tu parīkṣakāḥ // Brh_1,27.9 //	uBayoH api saMdigDam kitavAH tu parIkzakAH // Brh_1,27.9 //
   yadā vidveṣiṇas te tu tadā rājā vicārayet // Brh_1,27.10 //	yadA vidveziNaH te tu tadA rAjA vicArayet // Brh_1,27.10 //
   evaṃ vādikṛtān vādān prapaśyet pratyahaṃ nṛpaḥ /	evam vAdi-kRtAn vAdAn prapaSyet pratyaham nRpaH /
   nṛpāśrayās tathā cānye vidvadbhir brāhmaṇaiḥ saha // Brh_1,27.11 //	nRpa-ASrayAH taTA ca-anye vidvadBiH brAhmaNEH saha // Brh_1,27.11 //
   [Brh_1,28 samāhvayaḥ]	[Brh_1,28 samAhvayaH]
   [Brh_1,28.]	[Brh-_1,28.]
   anyonyaparigṛhītāḥ pakṣimeṣavṛṣādayaḥ /	anyonya-parigRhItAH pakzi-meza-vRza-AdayaH /
   praharante kṛtapaṇās taṃ vadanti samāhvayam // Brh_1,28.1 //	praharante kRta-paNAH tam vadanti samAhvayam // Brh_1,28.1 //
   dvandvayuddhena yaḥ kaścid avasādam avāpnuyāt /	dvandva-yudDena yaH kaScid avasAdam avApnuyAt /
   tatsvāminā paṇo deyo yas tatra parikalpitaḥ // Brh_1,28.2 //	tad-svAminA paNaH deyaH yaH tatra parikalpitaH // Brh_1,28.2 //
   [Brh_1,29 prakīrṇakam]	[Brh_1,29 prakIrNakam]
   [Brh_1,29.]	[Brh-_1,29.]
   eṣa vādikṛtaḥ prokto vyavahāraḥ samāsataḥ /	eza vA-Adi-kRtaH proktaH vyavahAraH samAsatas /
   nṛpāśrayaṃ pravakṣyāmi vyavahāraṃ prakīrṇakam // Brh_1,29.1 //	nRpa-ASrayam pravakzyAmi vyavahAram prakIrNakam // Brh_1,29.1 //
   vāgdhigdaṇḍaṃ vadhaṃ caiva caturdhā kalpitaṃ damam /	vAgDigdaNxam vaDam ca-eva caturDA kalpitam damam /
   puruṣaṃ doṣavibhavaṃ jñātvā saṃparikalpayet // Brh_1,29.2 //	puruzam doza-viBavam jQAtvA saMparikalpayet // Brh_1,29.2 //
   suvarṇaśatam ekaṃ tu vadhārho daṇḍam arhati /	suvarNa-Satam ekam tu vaDa-arhaH daNxam arhati /
   aṅgacchede tadardhaṃ tu vivāse pañcaviṃśatim // Brh_1,29.3 //	aFga=-Cede tad-arDam tu vivAse paQcaviMSatim // Brh_1,29.3 //
   hastāṅghriliṅganayanaṃ jihvākarṇau ca nāsikā /	hasta-aFGri-liFga-nayanam jihvA-karNO ca nAsikA /
   jihvā pādārdhasaṃdaṃśa- lalāṭauṣṭhagudaṃ kaṭiḥ // Brh_1,29.4 //	jihvA pAda-arDa-saMdaMSa lalAwa-ozWa-gudam kawiH // Brh_1,29.4 //
   sthānāny etāni daṇḍasya nirdiṣṭāni caturdaśa /	sTAnAni etAni daNxasya nirdizwAni caturdaSa /
   lalāṭāṅko brāhmaṇasya nānyo daṇḍo vidhīyate // Brh_1,29.5 //	lalAwa-aFkaH brAhmaNasya na-anyaH daNxaH viDIyate // Brh_1,29.5 //
   adhārmikāṃs tribhir nyāyair nigṛhṇīyāt prayatnataḥ /	aDArmikAn triBiH nyAyEH nigRhNIyAt prayatnataH /
   nirodhanena bandhena vividhena bhayena ca // Brh_1,29.6 //	niroDanena banDena viviDena Bayena ca // Brh_1,29.6 //
   vedhenāpi yadā tv etān nigṛhītuṃ na śaknuyāt /	veDena-api yadA tu etAn nigRhItum na SaknuyAt /
   tadaiṣu sarvam apy etat prayuñjīta catuṣṭayam // Brh_1,29.7 //	tadA-ezu sarvam api etat prayuQjIta catuzwayam // Brh_1,29.7 //
   vāgdaṇḍaṃ prathamaṃ kuryād dhigdaṇḍaṃ tadanantaram /	vAgdaNxam praTamam kuryAt DigdaNxam tad-anantaram /
   tṛtīyaṃ dhanadaṇḍaṃ tu vadhadaṇḍam ataḥ param // Brh_1,29.8 //	tRtIyam Dana-daNxam tu vaDa-daNxam atas param // Brh_1,29.8 //
   bandhanāni ca sarvāṇi rājamārge niveśayet /	banDanAni ca sarvANi rAjamArge niveSayet /
   duḥkhitā yatra dṛśyante vikṛtāḥ pāpakāriṇaḥ // Brh_1,29.9 //	duHKitAH yatra dRSyante vikRtAH pApa-kAriNaH // Brh_1,29.9 //
   daśamāṃśaṃ hared arthaṃ pañcamaṃ sarvam eva vā /	daSama-aMSam haret arTam paQcamam sarvam eva vA /
   mṛtasya vittād ādadyād ajñātiḥ śavadahakaḥ // Brh_1,29.10 //	mRtasya vittAt AdadyAt ajQAtiH Sava-dahakaH // Brh_1,29.10 //
   bahurakṣasya daśamam alparakṣasya pañcamam /	bahu-rakzasya daSamam alpa-rakzasya paQcamam /
   aputrapitṛbhāryasya sarvam eveti śaunakaḥ // Brh_1,29.11 //	aputra-pitR-BAryasya sarvam eva-iti SOnakaH // Brh_1,29.11 //
   ṣaḍbhāgas taraśulkaṃ ca gate deyas tathaiva ca /	zaz-BAgaH taraSulkam ca gate deyaH taTA-eva ca /
   saṃgrāmacaurabhedī ca sasyaghātanakṛt tathā // Brh_1,29.12 //	saMgrAma-cOra-BedI ca sasya-GAta-na-kRt taTA // Brh_1,29.12 //
   niṣkṛtīnām akaraṇaṃ ājñāsedhavyatikramaḥ /	nizkRtInAm akaraNam AjQA-seDa-vyatikramaH /
   varṇāśramāṇāṃ lopaś ca varṇasaṃkaralopanam // Brh_1,29.13 //	varNa-ASramANAm lopaH ca varNa-saMkara-lopanam // Brh_1,29.13 //
   nidhir niṣkulavittaṃ ca daridrasya dhanāgamaḥ /	niDiH nizkula-vittam ca daridrasya Dana-AgamaH /
   anāmnātāni kāryāṇi kriyāvādāś ca vādinām // Brh_1,29.14 //	anAmnAtAni kAryANi kriyA-vAdAH ca vAdinAm // Brh_1,29.14 //
   prakṛtīnāṃ prakopaś ca saṃketaś ca parasparam /	prakRtInAm prakopaH ca saMketaH ca parasparam /
   aśāstravihitaṃ yac ca prajāyāṃ saṃprakīrtyate // Brh_1,29.15 //	aSAstra-vihitam yat ca prajAyAm saMprakIrtyate // Brh_1,29.15 //
   sākṣisabhyārthasannānāṃ dūṣaṇe darśanaṃ punaḥ /	sAkzi-saBya-arTa-sannAnAm dUzaNe darSanam punar /
   svavācaiva jitānāṃ tu noktaḥ paunarbhāvo vidhiḥ // Brh_1,29.16 //	sva-vAcA-eva jitAnAm tu na-uktaH pOnarBAvaH viDiH // Brh_1,29.16 //

   vedārthopanibaddhatvāt prādhānyaṃ tu manoḥ smṛtam /	veda-arTa-upanibadDa-tvAt prADAnyam tu manoH smRtam /
